 77            //* user-defined the location of formats
 78            //LIBRARY DD DISP=SHR,DSN=XXXX.XXXXXXX
 79            //*user-defined the location of macros

 81            //*the location of person-level file
 82            //IN1 DD DISP=SHR,DSN=XXXX.PERSON
 83            //*the location of the diagnosis file
 84            //IN2 DD DISP=SHR,DSN=XXXX.DIAG
 85            //*the location of the file containing all coefficients
 86            //INCOEF DD DISP=SHR,DSN=XXXX.HCCCOEFN
 87            //*the output file containing person-level scores

 89            //    DSN=XXX.V2824T2P.PERSON,

 91            //SYSIN  DD *

 95           on your PC in a libname/filename statement.
 96         
 97           LIBNAME LIBRARY "location of formats";
 98           FILENAME IN0 "location of macros";
 99           LIBNAME  IN1 "location of person-level file";
 100          LIBNAME  IN2 "location of diagnosis file";
 101          LIBNAME  INCOEF "location of the coefficients file";
 102          LIBNAME  OUT "location for the output file";
 103          */

 116        
 117         ***********************************************************************
 118         *
 119         *   DESCRIPTION:
 120         *
 121         * V2824T2P program creates 115 HCC variables Version 28
 122         * (&HCCV28_list115) and nine score variables for each person who is
 123         * present in a person file (supplied by user).
 124         * If a person has at least one diagnosis in DIAG file (supplied by
 125         * user) then HCC variables are created, otherwise HCCs are set to 0.
 126         * Score variables are created using coefficients from 9 final models:
 127         *  1) Community NonDual Aged
 128         *  2) Community NonDual Disabled
 129         *  3) Community Full Benefit Dual Aged
 130         *  4) Community Full Benefit Dual Disabled
 131         *  5) Community Partial Benefit Dual Aged
 132         *  6) Community Partial Benefit Dual Disabled
 133         *  7) Long Term Institutional
 134         *  8) New Enrollees
 135         *  9) SNP New Enrollees
 136         *
 137         * Assumptions about input files:
 138         *   - both files are sorted by person ID
 139         *
 140         *   - person level file has the following variables:
 141         *     :&IDVAR    - person ID variable (it is a macro parameter, MBI
 142         *                  for Medicare data)
 143         *     :DOB       - date of birth
 144         *     :SEX       - sex
 145         *     :OREC      - original reason for entitlement
 146         *     :LTIMCAID  - Medicaid dummy variable for LTI (payment year)
 147         *     :NEMCAID   - Medicaid dummy variable for new enrollees (payment
 148         *                  year)
 149         *
 150         *   - diagnosis level file has the following vars:
 151         *     :&IDVAR  - person ID variable (it is a macro parameter, MBI for
 152         *                Medicare data)
 153         *     :DIAG    - diagnosis
 154         *
 155         * The program supplies parameters to a main macro %V2824T2M that calls
 156         * other external macros specific to V28 model HCCs:
 157         *
 158         *      %AGESEXV2   - create age/sex, originally disabled, disabled vars
 159         *      %V28I0ED2   - perform edits to ICD10 diagnosis
 160         *      %V28115L3   - assign labels to HCCs
 161         *      %V28115H1   - set HCC=0 according to hierarchies
 162         *      %SCOREVAR   - calculate a score variable
 163         *
 164         * Program steps:
 165         *         step1: include external macros
 166         *         step2: define internal macro variables
 167         *         step3: merge person and diagnosis files outputting one
 168         *                record per person for each input person level record
 169         *         step3.1: declaration section
 170         *         step3.2: bring regression coefficients
 171         *         step3.3: merge person and diagnosis file
 172         *         step3.4: for the first record for a person set CC to 0
 173         *                  and calculate age
 174         *         step3.5: if there are any diagnoses for a person
 175         *                  then do the following:
 176         *                   - perform ICD10 edits using V28I0ED2 macro
 177         *                   - create CC using provided format
 178         *                   - create additional CC using additional formats
 179         *         step3.6: for the last record for a person do the
 180         *                  following:
 181         *                   - create demographic variables needed
 182         *                     for regressions (macro AGESEXV2)
 183         *                   - create HCC using hierarchies (macro V28115H1)
 184         *                   - create HCC interaction variables
 185         *                   - create HCC and DISABL interaction variables
 186         *                   - set HCCs and interaction vars to zero if there
 187         *                     are no diagnoses for a person
 188         *                   - create scores for community models
 189         *                   - create score for institutional model
 190         *                   - create score for new enrollee model
 191         *                   - create score for SNP new enrollee model
 192         *         step4: data checks and proc contents
 193         *
 194         *   USER CUSTOMIZATION:
 195         *
 196         * A user must supply 2 files with the variables described above and
 197         * set the following parameters:
 198         *      INP      - SAS input person dataset
 199         *      IND      - SAS input diagnosis dataset
 200         *      OUTDATA  - SAS output dataset
 201         *      IDVAR    - name of person ID variable (MBI for medicare data)
 202         *      KEEPVAR  - variables to keep in the output dataset
 203         *      SEDITS   - a switch that controls whether to perform MCE edits
 204         *                 on ICD10: 1-YES, 0-NO
 205         *      DATE_ASOF- reference date to calculate age. Set to February 1
 206         *                 of the payment year for consistency with CMS
 207         ***********************************************************************;
 208        
 209         %LET INPUTVARS=%STR(SEX DOB LTIMCAID NEMCAID OREC);

 212         %LET DEMVARS  =%STR(AGEF ORIGDS DISABL
